Vejam se entendem porque não posso tolerar este simbolo (foice e martelo) e Marx. São 9 minutos de documentário muito interessante. Este horror foi praticado em nome do socialismo, e é incompreensível que ainda existam pessoas instruidas que defendem isto ou se fazem de louco, dizendo que é mentira!! O simbolo do comunismo é mais abominável que o simbolo do Nazismo. Enquanto o simbolo do nazismo foi uma usurpação de um simbolo oriental milenar, o simbolo do comunismo foi inventado no início do século XX, e sob este simbolo e respectiva ideologia se praticou os crimes hediondos em uma escala nunca vista na história antes!

With the aurora borealis flaming coldly overhead, or the stars leaping in the frost dance, and the land numb and frozen under its pall of snow, this song of the huskies might have been the defiance of life, only it was pitched in minor key, with long-drawn wailings and half-sobs, and was more the pleading of life, the articulate travail of existence. It was an old song, old as the breed itself--one of the first songs of the younger world in a day when songs were sad. It was invested with the woe of unnumbered generations, this plaint by which Buck was so strangely stirred. When he moaned and sobbed, it was with the pain of living that was of old the pain of his wild fathers, and the fear and mystery of the cold and dark that was to them fear and mystery. And that he should be stirred by it marked the completeness with which he harked back through the ages of fire and roof to the raw beginnings of life in the howling ages. Jack London - The Call of the Wild
